    Public Function PieceToMove(ByVal Piece)

        If Piece = 11 Then

            Return WhitePawn1

        ElseIf Piece = 12 Then

            Return WhitePawn2

        ElseIf Piece = 13 Then

            Return WhitePawn3

        ElseIf Piece = 14 Then

            Return WhitePawn4

        ElseIf Piece = 15 Then

            Return WhitePawn5

        ElseIf Piece = 16 Then

            Return WhitePawn6

        ElseIf Piece = 17 Then

            Return WhitePawn7

        ElseIf Piece = 18 Then

            Return WhitePawn8

        ElseIf Piece = 21 Then

            Return WhiteRook1

        ElseIf Piece = 22 Then

            Return WhiteRook2

        ElseIf Piece = 31 Then

            Return WhiteKnight1

        ElseIf Piece = 32 Then

            Return WhiteKnight2

        ElseIf Piece = 33 Then

            Return WhiteKnight3

        ElseIf Piece = 41 Then

            Return WhiteBishop1

        ElseIf Piece = 42 Then

            Return WhiteBishop2

        ElseIf Piece = 51 Then

            Return WhiteQueen1

        ElseIf Piece = 52 Then

            Return WhiteQueen2

        ElseIf Piece = 60 Then

            Return WhiteKing

        ElseIf Piece = 71 Then

            Return WhiteRookie1

        ElseIf Piece = 72 Then

            Return WhiteRookie2

        ElseIf Piece = -11 Then

            Return BlackPawn1

        ElseIf Piece = -12 Then

            Return BlackPawn2

        ElseIf Piece = -13 Then

            Return BlackPawn3

        ElseIf Piece = -14 Then

            Return BlackPawn4

        ElseIf Piece = -15 Then

            Return BlackPawn5

        ElseIf Piece = -16 Then

            Return BlackPawn6

        ElseIf Piece = -17 Then

            Return BlackPawn7

        ElseIf Piece = -18 Then

            Return BlackPawn8

        ElseIf Piece = -21 Then

            Return BlackRook1

        ElseIf Piece = -22 Then

            Return BlackRook2

        ElseIf Piece = -31 Then

            Return BlackKnight1

        ElseIf Piece = -32 Then

            Return BlackKnight2

        ElseIf Piece = -33 Then

            Return BlackKnight3

        ElseIf Piece = -41 Then

            Return BlackBishop1

        ElseIf Piece = -42 Then

            Return BlackBishop2

        ElseIf Piece = -51 Then

            Return BlackQueen1

        ElseIf Piece = -52 Then

            Return BlackQueen2

        ElseIf Piece = -60 Then

            Return BlackKing

        ElseIf Piece = -71 Then

            Return BlackRookie1

        ElseIf Piece = -72 Then

            Return BlackRookie2

        Else

            MsgBox("PieceToMove Function Error " & Piece)

        End If

    End Function

    Public Sub ThreatenedPieces(ThreatenedPiece As Integer)

        If ThreatenedPiece = 11 Then

            WhitePawn1.Cursor = Cursors.Hand

            WhitePawn1.Image = Take.InitialImage

        ElseIf ThreatenedPiece = 12 Then

            WhitePawn2.Cursor = Cursors.Hand

            WhitePawn2.Image = Take.InitialImage

        ElseIf ThreatenedPiece = 13 Then

            WhitePawn3.Cursor = Cursors.Hand

        BlackKnight3.Image = BlackKnight3.InitialImage

        BlackBishop2.Image = BlackBishop2.InitialImage
        BlackQueen1.Image = BlackQueen1.InitialImage
        BlackQueen2.Image = BlackQueen2.InitialImage
        BlackKing.Image = BlackKing.InitialImage

    End Sub

    Public Sub InitialImageForWhite()

        WhitePawn1.Image = WhitePawn1.InitialImage
        WhitePawn2.Image = WhitePawn2.InitialImage
        WhitePawn3.Image = WhitePawn3.InitialImage
        WhitePawn4.Image = WhitePawn4.InitialImage
        WhitePawn5.Image = WhitePawn5.InitialImage
        WhitePawn6.Image = WhitePawn6.InitialImage
        WhitePawn7.Image = WhitePawn7.InitialImage
        WhitePawn8.Image = WhitePawn8.InitialImage
        WhiteRook1.Image = WhiteRook1.InitialImage
        WhiteRook2.Image = WhiteRook2.InitialImage
        WhiteRookie1.Image = WhiteRookie1.InitialImage
        WhiteRookie2.Image = WhiteRookie2.InitialImage
        WhiteKnight1.Image = WhiteKnight1.InitialImage
        WhiteKnight2.Image = WhiteKnight2.InitialImage
        WhiteKnight3.Image = WhiteKnight3.InitialImage
        WhiteBishop1.Image = WhiteBishop1.InitialImage
        WhiteBishop2.Image = WhiteBishop2.InitialImage
        WhiteQueen1.Image = WhiteQueen1.InitialImage
        WhiteQueen2.Image = WhiteQueen2.InitialImage
        WhiteKing.Image = WhiteKing.InitialImage

    End Sub



    Private Sub WhitePawn1_Click(sender As Object, e As MouseEventArgs) Handles WhitePawn1.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If e.Button = MouseButtons.Left Then

            If WhiteTurn = True Then

                Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                SelectedPiece = 11

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 11 Then

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 - 1)

                            End If

                            If counter1 = 7 Then

                                If Board(counter1 - 2, counter2) = 0 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 - 2)

                                End If

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf WhitePawn1.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

                NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 11 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = WhitePawn1.Location

                            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                            WhiteTurn = True

                            WhitePawn1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                            Call HandCursorForWhite()

                            WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                            If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 11 And counter1 = 1 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If WhiteQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 51

                            WhiteQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf WhiteQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 52

                            WhiteQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhitePawn1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = 11 And counter1 <> 1 Then

                        TempLocation = (PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2))).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 11 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= 11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= 11 Then

                            NumberOfWhitePawns -= 3

                            If WhiteRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf WhiteRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = True And NumberOfWhitePawns = 1 Then

                        WhitePawn1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhiteKnight3.Visible = True

                        WhiteKnight3.Location = New Point(WhitePawn1.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = False

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = 11 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = 33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 51

                            WhiteQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf WhiteQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 52

                            WhiteQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhitePawn4.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = 14 And counter1 <> 1 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 14 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= 11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= 11 Then

                            NumberOfWhitePawns -= 3

                            If WhiteRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf WhiteRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = True And NumberOfWhitePawns = 1 Then

                        WhitePawn4.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhiteKnight3.Visible = True

                        WhiteKnight3.Location = New Point(WhitePawn4.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = False

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = 14 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = 33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub WhitePawn5_Click(sender As Object, e As MouseEventArgs) Handles WhitePawn5.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If e.Button = MouseButtons.Left Then

            If WhiteTurn = True Then

                Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                SelectedPiece = 15

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 15 Then

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 - 1)

                            End If

                            If counter1 = 7 Then

                                If Board(counter1 - 2, counter2) = 0 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 - 2)

                                End If

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf WhitePawn5.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

                NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 15 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = WhitePawn5.Location

                            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                            WhiteTurn = True

                            WhitePawn5.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                            Call HandCursorForWhite()

                            WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                            If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 15 And counter1 = 1 Then

                        NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If WhiteQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 51

                            WhiteQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf WhiteQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 52

                            WhiteQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhitePawn5.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = 15 And counter1 <> 1 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 15 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= 11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= 11 Then

                            NumberOfWhitePawns -= 3

                            If WhiteRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf WhiteRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = True And NumberOfWhitePawns = 1 Then

                        WhitePawn5.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhiteKnight3.Visible = True

                        WhiteKnight3.Location = New Point(WhitePawn5.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = False

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn5.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = 15 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = 33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf WhitePawn8.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

                NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 18 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = WhitePawn8.Location

                            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                            WhiteTurn = True

                            WhitePawn8.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                            Call HandCursorForWhite()

                            WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                            If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 18 And counter1 = 1 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If WhiteQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 51

                            WhiteQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf WhiteQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 52

                            WhiteQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            WhiteQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            WhiteQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfWhitePawns -= 1

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhitePawn8.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = 18 And counter1 <> 1 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = 18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= 11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= 18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= 11 Then

                            NumberOfWhitePawns -= 3

                            If WhiteRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf WhiteRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                WhiteRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                WhiteRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                WhiteRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = 72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = True And NumberOfWhitePawns = 1 Then

                        WhitePawn8.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        WhiteKnight3.Visible = True

                        WhiteKnight3.Location = New Point(WhitePawn8.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = False

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhitePawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = 18 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = 33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub BlackPawn1_Click(sender As Object, e As MouseEventArgs) Handles BlackPawn1.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If e.Button = MouseButtons.Left Then

            If WhiteTurn = False Then

                Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                SelectedPiece = -11

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -11 Then

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 1)

                            End If

                            If counter1 = 2 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2) = 0 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 2)

                                End If

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf BlackPawn1.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece > 0 Then

                NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -11 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = BlackPawn1.Location

                            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                            WhiteTurn = False

                            BlackPawn1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                            Call HandCursorForBlack()

                            BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                            If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -11 And counter1 = 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If BlackQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -51

                            BlackQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf BlackQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -52

                            BlackQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackPawn1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = -11 And counter1 <> 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -11 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= -11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= -11 Then

                            NumberOfBlackPawns -= 3

                            If BlackRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf BlackRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = False And NumberOfBlackPawns = 1 Then

                        BlackPawn1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackKnight3.Visible = True

                        BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(BlackPawn1.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = -11 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = -33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

                            End If

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf BlackRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = False And NumberOfBlackPawns = 1 Then

                        BlackPawn3.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackKnight3.Visible = True

                        BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(BlackPawn3.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn3.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn3.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn3.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = -13 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = -33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub BlackPawn4_Click(sender As Object, e As MouseEventArgs) Handles BlackPawn4.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If e.Button = MouseButtons.Left Then

            If WhiteTurn = False Then

                Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                SelectedPiece = -14

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -14 Then

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 1)

                            End If

                            If counter1 = 2 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2) = 0 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 2)

                                End If

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf BlackPawn4.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece > 0 Then

                NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -14 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = BlackPawn4.Location

                            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                            WhiteTurn = False

                            BlackPawn4.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                            Call HandCursorForBlack()

                            BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                            If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -14 And counter1 = 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If BlackQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -51

                            BlackQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf BlackQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -52

                            BlackQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackPawn4.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = -14 And counter1 <> 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -14 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= -11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= -11 Then

                            NumberOfBlackPawns -= 3

                            If BlackRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf BlackRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = False And NumberOfBlackPawns = 1 Then

                        BlackPawn4.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackKnight3.Visible = True

                        BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(BlackPawn4.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn4.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = -14 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = -33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub BlackPawn5_Click(sender As Object, e As MouseEventArgs) Handles BlackPawn5.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If e.Button = MouseButtons.Left Then

            If WhiteTurn = False Then

                Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                SelectedPiece = -15

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -15 Then

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 1)

                            End If

                            If counter1 = 2 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2) = 0 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 2)

                                End If

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf BlackPawn5.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece > 0 Then

                NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                            End If

                    Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then
