                                BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -17 And counter1 = 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If BlackQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -51

                            BlackQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf BlackQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -52

                            BlackQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackPawn7.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = -17 And counter1 <> 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -17 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= -11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= -11 Then

                            NumberOfBlackPawns -= 3

                            If BlackRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf BlackRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = False And NumberOfBlackPawns = 1 Then

                        BlackPawn7.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackKnight3.Visible = True

                        BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(BlackPawn7.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn7.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = -17 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = -33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub BlackPawn8_Click(sender As Object, e As MouseEventArgs) Handles BlackPawn8.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If e.Button = MouseButtons.Left Then

            If WhiteTurn = False Then

                Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                SelectedPiece = -18

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -18 Then

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 1)

                            End If

                            If counter1 = 2 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2) = 0 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 * 10) + counter1 + 2)

                                End If

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 + 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 9 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 + 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, counter2 - 1) = 0 And counter2 <> 2 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(((counter2 - 1) * 10) + counter1)

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            ElseIf BlackPawn8.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece > 0 Then

                NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

                For counter1 = 1 To 8

                    For counter2 = 1 To 10

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -18 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = BlackPawn8.Location

                            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                            WhiteTurn = False

                            BlackPawn8.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                            Call HandCursorForBlack()

                            BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                            If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        End If

                    Next

                Next

            End If

        ElseIf e.Button = MouseButtons.Right Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -18 And counter1 = 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If BlackQueen1.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -51

                            BlackQueen1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen1.Visible = True

                        ElseIf BlackQueen2.Size.Height = 31 Then

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = -52

                            BlackQueen2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                            BlackQueen2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                            BlackQueen2.Visible = True

                        End If

                        NumberOfBlackPawns -= 1

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackPawn8.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    ElseIf Board(counter1, counter2) = -18 And counter1 <> 8 Then

                        TempLocation = PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Location

                        If Board(counter1, counter2) = -18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) <= -11 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) >= -18 And Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) <= -11 Then

                            NumberOfBlackPawns -= 3

                            If BlackRookie1.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie1.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie1.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie1.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -71

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            ElseIf BlackRookie2.Size.Height = 50 Then

                                BlackRookie2.Size = New Size(100, 100)

                                BlackRookie2.Location = New Point(TempLocation)

                                BlackRookie2.Visible = True

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                PieceToMove(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2)).Visible = False

                                Board(counter1, counter2) = -72

                                Board(counter1 + 1, counter2) = 0

                                Board(counter1 - 1, counter2) = 0

                            End If

                        End If

                    ElseIf WhiteTurn = False And NumberOfBlackPawns = 1 Then

                        BlackPawn8.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        BlackKnight3.Visible = True

                        BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(BlackPawn8.Location)

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackPawn8.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                        For counter3 = 1 To 8

                            For counter4 = 1 To 10

                                If Board(counter3, counter4) = -18 Then

                                    Board(counter3, counter4) = -33

                                End If

                            Next

                        Next

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub



    Private Sub WhiteRook1_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles WhiteRook1.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = True Then

            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

            SelectedPiece = 21

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 21 Then

                        If counter1 <> 8 Then

                            Temp1 = counter1

                            Do

                                If Temp1 < 8 Then

                                    Temp1 += 1

                                End If

                                If Board(Temp1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(counter2 * 10 + Temp1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(Temp1, counter2) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 8

                            If Board(Temp1, counter2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(Temp1, counter2))

                            End If

                            If counter2 <> 9 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter1 <> 1 Then

                            Temp1 = counter1

                            Do

                                If Temp1 > 1 Then

                                    Temp1 -= 1

                                End If

                                If Board(Temp1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(counter2 * 10 + Temp1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(Temp1, counter2) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 1

                            If Board(Temp1, counter2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(Temp1, counter2))

                            End If

                            If counter2 <> 2 Then

                                If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter2 <> 2 Then

                            Temp1 = counter2

                            Do

                                If Temp1 > 2 Then

                                    Temp1 -= 1

                                End If

                                If Board(counter1, Temp1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(Temp1 * 10 + counter1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(counter1, Temp1) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 2

                            If Temp1 = 2 And Board(counter1, 1) < 0 And Board(counter1, 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                            If counter1 <> 8 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter2 <> 9 Then

                            Temp1 = counter2

                            Do

                                If Temp1 < 9 Then

                                    Temp1 += 1

                                End If

                                If Board(counter1, Temp1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(Temp1 * 10 + counter1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(counter1, Temp1) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 9

                            If Temp1 = 9 And Board(counter1, 10) < 0 And Board(counter1, 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, 10))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                            If counter1 <> 1 Then

                                If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf WhiteRook1.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                Next

            Next

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 21 Then

                        PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = WhiteRook1.Location

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        WhiteRook1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        Call HandCursorForWhite()

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhiteRook1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhiteRook1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhiteRook1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                                If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf WhiteRook2.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                        PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = WhiteRook2.Location

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                            WhiteRook2.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhiteRook2.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhiteRook2.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

                                End If

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackRook1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackRook1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackRook1.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub BlackRook2_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles BlackRook2.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = False Then

            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

            SelectedPiece = -22

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -22 Then

                        If counter1 <> 8 Then

                            Temp1 = counter1

                            Do

                                If Temp1 < 8 Then

                                    Temp1 += 1

                                End If

                                If Board(Temp1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(counter2 * 10 + Temp1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(Temp1, counter2) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 8

                            If Board(Temp1, counter2) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(Temp1, counter2))

                            End If

                            If counter2 <> 9 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter1 <> 1 Then

                            Temp1 = counter1

                            Do

                                If Temp1 > 1 Then

                                    Temp1 -= 1

                                End If

                                If Board(Temp1, counter2) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(counter2 * 10 + Temp1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(Temp1, counter2) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 1

                            If Board(Temp1, counter2) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(Temp1, counter2))

                            End If

                            If counter2 <> 2 Then

                                If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter2 <> 2 Then

                            Temp1 = counter2

                            Do

                                If Temp1 > 2 Then

                                    Temp1 -= 1

                                End If

                                If Board(counter1, Temp1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(Temp1 * 10 + counter1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(counter1, Temp1) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 2

                            If Temp1 = 2 And Board(counter1, 1) > 0 And Board(counter1, 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                            If counter1 <> 8 Then

                                If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter2 <> 9 Then

                            Temp1 = counter2

                            Do

                                If Temp1 < 9 Then

                                    Temp1 += 1

                                End If

                                If Board(counter1, Temp1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(Temp1 * 10 + counter1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(counter1, Temp1) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 9

                            If Temp1 = 9 And Board(counter1, 10) > 0 And Board(counter1, 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, 10))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                            If counter1 <> 1 Then

                                If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                                End If

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf BlackRook2.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece > 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                Next

            Next

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -22 Then

                        PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = BlackRook2.Location

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                        WhiteTurn = False

                        BlackRook2.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        Call HandCursorForBlack()

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackRook2.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackRook2.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackRook2.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub



    Private Sub WhiteRookie1_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles WhiteRookie1.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = True Then

            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                                    Temp1 += 1

                                End If

                                End If

                                End If

                            If Board(Temp1, counter2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(Temp1, counter2))

                            End If

                        End If

                        If counter2 <> 2 Then

                            Temp1 = counter2

                            Do

                                If Temp1 > 2 Then

                                    Temp1 -= 1

                                End If

                                If Board(counter1, Temp1) = 0 Then

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(Temp1 * 10 + counter1)

                                End If

                            Loop Until Board(counter1, Temp1) <> 0 Or Temp1 = 2

                            If Temp1 = 2 And Board(counter1, 1) < 0 And Board(counter1, 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, 1))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                        End If

                                    Temp1 += 1

                                End If

                                    Call ShowAllPossibleMoves(Temp1 * 10 + counter1)

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, 10))

                            End If

                            If Board(counter1, Temp1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1, Temp1))

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf WhiteRookie1.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                Next

            Next

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 71 Then

                        PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = WhiteRookie1.Location

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        WhiteRookie1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        Call HandCursorForWhite()

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhiteRookie1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub WhiteKnight1_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles WhiteKnight1.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = True Then

            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()
            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

            SelectedPiece = 31

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 31 Then

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 - 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 - 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 2) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 2) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 2) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 2) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 + 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 + 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf WhiteKnight1.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                Next

            Next

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 31 Then

                        If counter2 = 1 Or counter2 = 10 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                            BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                            If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        Else

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = WhiteKnight1.Location

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                        End If

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        WhiteKnight1.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        Call HandCursorForWhite()

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhiteKnight1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            WhiteKnight1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 91)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            WhiteKnight1.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 165)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub

    Private Sub WhiteKnight2_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles WhiteKnight2.Click

        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = True Then

            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()
            Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

            SelectedPiece = 32

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 32 Then

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 - 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 - 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 2, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 2) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 + 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 2) * 10 + counter1 - 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 - 1, counter2 - 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 2) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 2) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 + 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 + 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1) < 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf WhiteKnight2.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece < 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                Next

            Next

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = 32 Then

                        If counter2 = 1 Or counter2 = 10 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                            BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                            If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                            ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        Else

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = WhiteKnight1.Location

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                        End If

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                        WhiteTurn = True

                        WhiteKnight2.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        Call HandCursorForWhite()

                        WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                        If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            WhiteKnight2.Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 128)

                        ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 2) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 + 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 2) * 10 + counter1 + 1)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 1, counter2 - 2))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 + 1) * 10 + counter1 + 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 + 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                        Try

                            If Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1) = 0 Then

                                Call ShowAllPossibleMoves((counter2 - 1) * 10 + counter1 + 2)

                            ElseIf Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1) > 0 Then

                                Call ThreatenedPieces(Board(counter1 + 2, counter2 - 1))

                            End If

                        Catch ex As Exception

                        End Try

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        ElseIf BlackKnight3.Cursor = Cursors.Hand And SelectedPiece > 0 Then

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                        Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                    End If

                Next

            Next

            For counter1 = 1 To 8

                For counter2 = 1 To 10

                    If Board(counter1, counter2) = -33 Then

                        If counter2 = 1 Or counter2 = 10 Then

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Size = New Size(31, 31)

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = 0

                            WhitePiecesTaken += 1

                            If WhitePiecesTaken > 6 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken <= 6 And WhitePiecesTaken > 0 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                            ElseIf WhitePiecesTaken > 12 And WhitePiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                                PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).Location = New Point(27 + (WhitePiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 580)

                            Else

                                MsgBox("WhitePiecesTaken Error")

                            End If

                        Else

                            PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = BlackKnight3.Location

                            Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece

                        End If

                        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()

                        WhiteTurn = False

                        BlackKnight3.Size = New Size(31, 31)

                        Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

                        Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

                        Call HandCursorForBlack()

                        BlackPiecesTaken += 1

                        If BlackPiecesTaken > 6 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 12 Then

                            BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 7) * 37, 543)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken <= 6 And BlackPiecesTaken > 0 Then

                            BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 1) * 37, 506)

                        ElseIf BlackPiecesTaken > 12 And BlackPiecesTaken <= 18 Then

                            BlackKnight3.Location = New Point(27 + (BlackPiecesTaken - 13) * 37, 508)

                        Else

                            MsgBox("BlackPiecesTaken Error")

                        End If

                    End If

                Next

            Next

        End If

    End Sub


    Private Sub PossibleMove_11_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles PossibleMove_11.Click

        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()
        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = True Then

            WhiteTurn = False

            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

            Call HandCursorForBlack()

        Else

            WhiteTurn = True

            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

            Call HandCursorForWhite()

        End If

        For counter1 = 1 To 8

            For counter2 = 1 To 10

                If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                    Board(counter1, counter2) = 0
                    Board(1, 1) = SelectedPiece
                    PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = New Point(PossibleMove_11.Location)

                    If Abs(SelectedPiece) >= 31 And Abs(SelectedPiece) <= 33 Then

                        If counter2 = 1 Or counter2 = 10 Then

                            'Knight wears a hood

                        Else

                            Try

                                If Board(2, 1) <> 0 And Board(0, 1) <> 0 And Board(1, 2) <> 0 And Board(1, 0) <> 0 Then

                                    MainEntranceElig = True

                                End If

                            Catch ex As Exception

                                MainEntranceElig = False

                            End Try

                            If MainEntranceElig = True Then

                                Try

                                    If Board(3, 1) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(2, 1)).Location = New Point(PieceToMove(Board(2, 1)).Location.X, PieceToMove(Board(2, 1)).Location.Y + 100)

                                        Board(3, 1) = Board(2, 1)
                                        Board(2, 1) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(2, 1) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(-1, 1) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(0, 1)).Location = New Point(PieceToMove(Board(0, 1)).Location.X, PieceToMove(Board(0, 1)).Location.Y - 100)

                                        Board(-1, 1) = Board(0, 1)
                                        Board(0, 1) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(0, 1) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(1, 3) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(1, 2)).Right += 100

                                        Board(1, 3) = Board(1, 2)
                                        Board(1, 2) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(1, 2) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(1, -1) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(1, 0)).Left += 100

                                        Board(1, -1) = Board(1, 0)
                                        Board(1, 0) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(1, 0) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                End If

            Next

        Next

    End Sub

                                    If Board(7, -1) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(7, 0)).Left += 100

                                        Board(7, -1) = Board(7, 0)
                                        Board(7, 0) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(7, 0) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                End If

            Next

        Next

    End Sub

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(6, 10) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(7, 12) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(7, 11)).Right += 100

                                        Board(7, 12) = Board(7, 11)
                                        Board(7, 11) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(7, 11) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(7, 8) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(7, 9)).Left += 100

                                        Board(7, 8) = Board(7, 9)
                                        Board(7, 9) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(7, 9) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                End If

            Next

        Next

    End Sub

    Private Sub PossibleMove_108_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs) Handles PossibleMove_108.Click

        Call HideAllPossibleMoves()
        Call InitialImageForBlack()
        Call InitialImageForWhite()

        If WhiteTurn = True Then

            WhiteTurn = False

            Call DefaultCursorForWhite()

            Call HandCursorForBlack()

        Else

            WhiteTurn = True

            Call DefaultCursorForBlack()

            Call HandCursorForWhite()

        End If

        For counter1 = 1 To 8

            For counter2 = 1 To 10

                If Board(counter1, counter2) = SelectedPiece Then

                    Board(counter1, counter2) = 0
                    Board(8, 10) = SelectedPiece
                    PieceToMove(SelectedPiece).location = New Point(PossibleMove_108.Location)

                    If Abs(SelectedPiece) >= 31 And Abs(SelectedPiece) <= 33 Then

                        If counter2 = 1 Or counter2 = 10 Then

                            'Knight wears a hood

                        Else

                            Try

                                If Board(9, 10) <> 0 And Board(7, 10) <> 0 And Board(8, 11) <> 0 And Board(8, 9) <> 0 Then

                                    MainEntranceElig = True

                                End If

                            Catch ex As Exception

                                MainEntranceElig = False

                            End Try

                            If MainEntranceElig = True Then

                                Try

                                    If Board(10, 10) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(9, 10)).Location = New Point(PieceToMove(Board(9, 10)).Location.X, PieceToMove(Board(9, 10)).Location.Y + 100)

                                        Board(10, 10) = Board(9, 10)
                                        Board(9, 10) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(9, 10) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(6, 10) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(7, 10)).Location = New Point(PieceToMove(Board(7, 10)).Location.X, PieceToMove(Board(7, 10)).Location.Y - 100)

                                        Board(6, 10) = Board(7, 10)
                                        Board(7, 10) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(7, 10) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(8, 12) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(8, 11)).Right += 100

                                        Board(8, 12) = Board(8, 11)
                                        Board(8, 11) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(8, 11) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                                Try

                                    If Board(8, 8) = 0 Then

                                        PieceToMove(Board(8, 9)).Left += 100

                                        Board(8, 8) = Board(8, 9)
                                        Board(8, 9) = 0

                                    Else

                                        Board(11, 11) = 0   'Cause an error to enter the Catch section

                                    End If

                                Catch ex As Exception

                                    'Piece in Board(8, 9) can't take the Knight in the next move

                                End Try

                            End If

                        End If

                    End If

                End If

            Next

        Next

    End Sub

End Class
